Originally developed as a biological weapon disguised as an aphrodisiac, CR-4CK was supposed to be used to distract enemy forces in times of war by putting them in a state of uncontrollable lust and preventing them from putting up any resistance when attacked. The results of the virus where however deemed to dangerous and thus the project prematurely got shut down altogether for the safety of humankind. The virus infiltrates it's hosts body, lying dormant and heightening their senses of arousal. What almost nobody knew however, not the people who originally created the virus, not the leaders of the facility and not the authorities, was that midway through the outbreak a strange mutation in the virus had occurred. With coordinated attacks and sophisticated tactics they were the lone reason that the last resistance in the facility eventually failed to hold off the outbreak.
